04/12/24, 7:02â€¯pm - Kanak Gupta AIDS: # Electronic Voting Machine in Python

# Define the candidates
candidates = {
    1: 'Candidate A',
    2: 'Candidate B',
    3: 'Candidate C'
}

# Initialize vote counts
votes = {1: 0, 2: 0, 3: 0}

# Function to display candidates
def display_candidates():
    print("\nCandidates:")
    for key, value in candidates.items():
        print(f"{key}. {value}")

# Function to vote
def cast_vote():
    display_candidates()
    try:
        choice = int(input("\nEnter the number corresponding to the candidate you want to vote for: "))
        if choice in candidates:
            votes[choice] += 1
            print(f"Vote casted successfully for {candidates[choice]}")
        else:
            print("Invalid choice. Please try again.")
    except ValueError:
        print("Invalid input. Please enter a valid number.")

# Function to show the result
def show_results():
    print("\nElection Results:")
    for key, value in votes.items():
        print(f"{candidates[key]}: {value} votes")
    
    # Determine the winner
    winner = max(votes, key=votes.get)
    print(f"\nThe winner is {candidates[winner]} with {votes[winner]} votes!")

# Main program
def voting_machine():
    print("Welcome to the Electronic Voting Machine")
    
    while True:
        print("\n1. Cast Vote")
        print("2. Show Results")
        print("3. Exit")
        try:
            option = int(input("\nEnter your choice: "))
            if option == 1:
                cast_vote()
            elif option == 2:
                show_results()
            elif option == 3:
                print("Exiting the voting machine.")
                break
            else:
                print("Invalid option. Please choose again.")
        except ValueError:
            print("Invalid input. Please enter a valid number.")

# Run the voting machine
if __name__ == "__main__":
    voting_machine()
